***стеснение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стеснение.html>стесне́ние</a> (15492)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">стесни́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stesnítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стеснение.html>стесне́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stesnénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стеснение.html>стесне́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стеснение.html>стесне́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стеснение.html>стесне́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>constraint, restraint</li>
<li>uneasiness, shyness</li>
<li>(feeling of) shame or shyness, standing on ceremony</li>
<li>difficulty in breathing</li></ol>

***стеснять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стеснять.html>стесня́ть</a> (19766)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">стесни́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stesnítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стеснять.html>стесня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stesnjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стесни́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put/lay restraint <i>(on)</i>, to hinder, to hamper
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стеснять.html>стесня́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:движение.html>движе́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stesnjátʹ</b> dvižénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hinder movements</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стеснять.html>стесня́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:расход.html>расхо́дах</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stesnjátʹ</b> sebjá v rasxódax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to restrict one's spending</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стеснять.html>стесня́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:расход.html>расхо́дах</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>stesnjátʹ</b> sebjá v rasxódax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to spend money lavishly</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to embarrass</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стесняться.html>стесня́ться</a> (3247)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стеснять.html>стесня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stesnjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стесняться.html>стесня́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stesnjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стесни́ться</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постесняться.html>постесня́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be uncomfortable</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to feel embarrassed</li>
<li>to be sparing <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + prepositional, with</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стесни́ться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stesnítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to crowd together
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стесни́ться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stesnítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be afraid, to ashamed to <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ infinitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постесняться.html>постесня́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">postesnjátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be afraid of <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ genitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постесняться.html>постесня́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">postesnjátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стеснять.html>стесня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stesnjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стимул.html>сти́мул</a> (15187)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стимул.html>сти́мул</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stímul</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стимул.html>сти́мула</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стимул.html>сти́мулы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стимул.html>сти́мулов</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стирать.html>стира́ть</a> (5969)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тира́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-tirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стирать.html>стира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стереть.html>стере́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to erase something from a surface</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тереть.html>тере́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">terétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably ultimately the same as etymology 1, but reinterpreted as an unprefixed verb.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стирать.html>стира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стереть.html>стере́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постирать.html>постира́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выстирать.html>вы́стирать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to clean, to wash cloth or clothes</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стираться.html>стира́ться</a> (25900)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стирать.html>стира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стираться.html>стира́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stirátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стереться.html>стере́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be obliterated/effaced, to rub away, to become obliterated
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стираться.html>стира́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:память.html>па́мяти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stirátʹsja</b> v pámjati</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be erased/effaced from memory</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стирать.html>стира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стирать.html>стира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стираться.html>стира́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stirátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">постира́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wash
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ткань.html>ткань</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хорошо́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стираться.html>стира́ется</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éta tkanʹ xorošó <b>stirájetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">this cloth washes well</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стирать.html>стира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">стиск-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stisk-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тиснуть.html>ти́снуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tísnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***стих.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стихи.html>стих</a> (8987)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">стихъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stixŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">стихъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stixŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">στίχος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stíkhos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">row, line, verse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стихи.html>стих</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stix</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стихи.html>стиха́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стихи.html>стихи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стихи.html>стихо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>verse</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biblical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> verse</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> poem, poems</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стихи.html>стих</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stix</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стихи.html>сти́ха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стихи.html>сти́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стихи.html>сти́хов</a></b>)

***стихать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стихать.html>стиха́ть</a> (10921)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стихнуть.html>сти́хнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stíxnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стихать.html>стиха́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stixátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стихнуть.html>сти́хнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to quiet down, to abate, to die down <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a storm, war, fighting, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
